The reason I take time to write reviews is because the most important part of doing business with any company is the Customer Service.  Like many online retailers, it can be difficult to get a human on the phone however they are VERY quick to respond to email and they truly STAND behind their product.  When you spend $100 on something, you hope a company will stand behind their product and customers.  The fact is they easily deserve 5 STARS due to their  Customer Service. They stand behind their product and Sam, the Customer Service person, delivered as promised.

As for the product, TouchUp Direct is the real deal and their paint was a perfect match.  I am saying this as someone who owns two Pearl White vehicles which require a 3 Stage Paint job.  For those Amateur DIYers, this was more difficult than expected.  The Base Coat from TouchUpDirect was SPOT ON however it's the mid coat, provides the sparkle look, was a bit difficult to blend.  Take their advice and PRACTICE... if not, you will end up making a huge mistake and this paint is expensive.  I attempted to fix a spot with paint from AutoZone and Advance Auto and the quality was terrible and the color was not even close.

I can't thank them enough for not "screwing" the customer like so many other online vendors. Great JOB!!< /Review>

My import mechanic told me they fit perfectly no bolt conversions or anything my tires do not rub, it was the exact look I was looking for and I couldn't have done it without Mario! Did I mention he gave me his cell?! I'll start off by saying that every time my wife and I have gone to California sun the staff is very friendly and helpful, and the machines are clean.

It's always a pleasant experience when we go into any of their locations.

However the communication from the corporate side was non-existent during the shutdown and reopening.

We were not alerted via email, call, or text about their closures but we assumed that they would be closing like most businesses. So that's not a big deal.

However we never received an email, call, or text when they reopened on May 25th.

We were charged for the month of June membership and that's how we found out they were open. So now we have missed out on March 20-31 which we paid for, and May 25-June 2 which we paid for. That's 20 days...about 2/3 of a month!

My wife and I pay over $100/month between the two of us. I would think we deserve a little communication. Or at the very least 20 days each of credit for tanning that we could have had we been notified.

So again the staff is friendly, the machines are clean, the communication sucks!!!< /text>

2</rating>
< text>
This is a warning for California Sun contracts!  Even though most of their salons are nice and clean and employees were friendly (therefore 2 stars);  dealing with the fine print in the contract turned out to be a nightmare!
I went to the Fair Oaks location prior to my Caribbean vacation for a month of tanning.  I was told I could cancel any time and there was no long term commitment.

Immediately, after signing up it was clear that the first month's payment did not count towards the month-to-month contract.

In my case, I was charged another month and since I went on my trip, they offered a "Stay and Save".  A monthly $5 charge will be billed to your account,  up to 12 months, until you are ready to re-activate.  The kicker is, that when you re-activate, you have to pay another month pro-rated, before they use the money in your account.
This, to me, is very deceptive and not worth the hassle.

If you are planning to use California Sun's services, sign up at the end of the month, for that month's prorated fee, and cancel prior to the 20th of the next month.  Make sure you do that in writing at the corporate office, because they won't let you cancel at the salon.< /text>

None< /Response>
<text>Great selection of new and older games. Helpful staff with a very knowledgeable owner. Literally thousands of board games, role playing games, card games, dice games, miniature war games, miniatures, dice, and gaming accessories for all types of gamers. The store is packed wall to wall, a definite must go and see. Especially if you like to see and feel before purchasing. The staff is happy to let you shop, look, and feel without pressure to buy. There is also in-store gaming of all sorts nearly everyday. Pathfinder and D&D on the weekends (even into the night), as well as card games (Magic the Gathering, Pokemon, etc), Star Wars X-Wing, and Hero Clix during the week. It is very local for those in Long Beach and the South Bay areas. Of course, since it is only 2 blocks off the Long Beach Freeway, it is pretty accessible to anyone in L.A., Orange, or San Bernardino Counties in California. They also do mail order and have an Ebay store for those not in the area. I cannot say enough good things about this store. They have been in business since 1974!!!< /text>< Gmap_id>
